 ief and ales ke west tu energy plant main dilli ke musiibat vaale kachare ko na sirf eendhan kii tarah istemaal kiya jaataa he, balki isse bijli banaakar gharon main supplai kii jaati he

 Friendship Day is celebrated on the first Sunday of August every year in memory of such true friends
 is saal dosti kaa yah tyohaar 4 agast ko manaaya ja rahaa he
 But have you ever wondered when and how this day started? is din ko friendship ke rup main sabase pehle kisne manaaya hoga
 If these questions also bother your mind, then after removing your problem, let us tell you when and how the beginning of celebrating Friendship Day happened
 friendship de kaa itihaas-friendship de kii shuruyaat saal 1935 main america se hui thi
 It is said that on the first Sunday of August, a person was killed by the US government
 jisaki yaad main uske ek dost ne aatmahatya kar lee thi
 After which the government decided to celebrate the first Sunday of August as Friendship Day from that day
 friendship de se judi kahaniyaan-kaha jaataa he ki saal 1930 main ek vyapaaree ne is din kii shuruuaat kii thi
 This merchant, named Joe Hall, kept a day for all people in which two friends could celebrate each day by giving cards to each other
 is khaas din ko manaane ke liye us vyapaaree ne 2 agast ke din ko chunaa
 Later many countries in Europe and Asia decided to celebrate Friendship Day, carrying on this tradition
 -friendship de se judi ek or kahani or itihaas sunne main aata he
 It is said that on 20 July 1958, Dr
 Raman Artemio proposed the idea of celebrating friendship day with his friends during a dinner party
 paragway main hui is ghatana ke baad vishwa main friendship de manaane kii parampara par khaasaa dhyaan diya gaya
